  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_25741f37-3e63-43c1-8e8d-f4681f9d4d72'
      });

  <span id="freeText1758230064135516719" style="display:none">She’s smart, she’s sassy and she’s sexy as hell - meet Tawny, aka “The Happy Spinster,” an auburn haired siren whose seductive style has set many a male heart racing in old Montreal. While at her local one Friday night, she meets Troy, a Texas cowboy whose smoldering good looks immediately ignite Tawny’s sexual craving. With a mutual attraction between them and a burning carnal desire within them, Tawny and Troy embark on an ardor filled night of sensational sex and passionate lovemaking but – will Tawny break the rules and fall in love with the handsome bronco buster? And is there a future for a woman from the city and a ranch hand from the Texas panhandle?</span>

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/643905811" />
    <a title="Dan McNeil" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/19131633-dan-mcneil"><img alt="Dan McNeil" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1406984424p2/19131633.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/643905811?book_show_action=true">Jun 17, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Dan McNeil" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Dan McNeil" href="/user/show/19131633-dan-mcneil">Dan McNeil</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer643905811" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9710515118838346188">I’m not a regular reader of erotica (actually, this is my first) so I wasn’t sure what to expect from Karena Marie’s “The Happy Spinster.” What I discovered, to my surprise, was a thoroughly enjoyable read about a woman who is very comfortable in her exceptionally seductive skin.<br/>It would be flippant to say that the heroine of this story is an “easy woman.” On the contrary, Tawny is a smart, vivacious and very sexy woman who is incredibly self-assured and is not afraid to go after what she wants </span>
  <span id="freeText9710515118838346188" style="display:none">I’m not a regular reader of erotica (actually, this is my first) so I wasn’t sure what to expect from Karena Marie’s “The Happy Spinster.” What I discovered, to my surprise, was a thoroughly enjoyable read about a woman who is very comfortable in her exceptionally seductive skin.<br />It would be flippant to say that the heroine of this story is an “easy woman.” On the contrary, Tawny is a smart, vivacious and very sexy woman who is incredibly self-assured and is not afraid to go after what she wants – and she does.<br />What I was really impressed with was that I never got the feeling that Tawny was, in any way, a "loose woman," so to speak. I think in less capable hands it could have been written that way but the author’s approach was so much more adept, appealing and, of course, erotic. I like Tawny, but not in that "50 Shades" way or whatever. I think she is an exceptional individual and pretty cool to boot – I certainly look forward to seeing more of her in the future. I recommend this excellent read.<br /></span>

          </span>

Tawny, the main character, or The Happy Spinster, is a woman that knows what she wants and goes after it!   <span id="freeText15350270203919154529" style="display:none">The Happy Spinster is spectacular! Erotic and hot, hot, hot! Tawny, the main character, or The Happy Spinster, is a woman that knows what she wants and goes after it! She finds a cowboy and wastes no time giving him a ride in a backseat that leaves him wanting more. The Happy Spinster is a secure, complete woman who takes her pleasure where she wants it! I have always wondered what my life would be like if I never met my husband. I would want to be just like Tawny. Great book about female empowerment and none of this BDSM stuff that every book has. If you do nott find yourself loving Tawny, then you do not like strong, free women. I would have given in 5 stars, but the ending did not go as I wanted it to.<br /><br /></span>

        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/982066313?book_show_action=true">Jun 30, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Kate" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Kate" href="/user/show/7232234-kate">Kate</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="did not like it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">did not like it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7232234-kate?shelf=awfulness">awfulness</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7232234-kate?shelf=didn-t-finish">didn-t-finish</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer982066313" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4561119254792198053">Bought the Kindle edition and stopped reading approx. 10 pages in. Here's why:<br/><br/><a class='jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction'>(view spoiler)</a><span class='spoilerContainer' style='display: none'>[
  <i>Almost like magic, Teresa's timing was perfect as she dropped the two shots down, before scurrying off to another customer. It gave Tawny a chance to see that Troy had beautiful green eyes. Up close, she could also see he was a good-looking man, and would look just as handsome in a designer suit as he did in the fine pair of Levis he was currently wearing.<br/>"Where I come from, it's the Man who buys the </i></span></span>
  <span id="freeText4561119254792198053" style="display:none">Bought the Kindle edition and stopped reading approx. 10 pages in. Here's why:<br /><br /><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[
  <i>Almost like magic, Teresa's timing was perfect as she dropped the two shots down, before scurrying off to another customer. It gave Tawny a chance to see that Troy had beautiful green eyes. Up close, she could also see he was a good-looking man, and would look just as handsome in a designer suit as he did in the fine pair of Levis he was currently wearing.<br />"Where I come from, it's the Man who buys the Lady a drink."<br />"Why, I will have to remember that, if I ever visit where you are from but since we are here, and the shots are ready, let's say we drink them up?" Tawny then lifted her glass and waited for the cowboy to do the same. As he lifted his class to her, she said "Cheers!"<br />They both downed their shots and Tawny took a sip of her beer. "So, I hear you are up here, from Texas, is it?"<br />"Yes I am! And what might your name be?"<br />"Oh, sorry, where are my manners! I am Tawny, and you are...?"<br />"Troy. It's nice to meet you."</i>
 <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br />I <b>hate</b> the writing. The poor editing I could get over having read some shocking Kindle books recently which had writing, characters and plots strong enough to allow me to gloss over it, but this is just terrible writing. <br /><br />Introducing the main character before you actually introduce him. Check. <br />Slinging together prose that make absolutely no sense except to bulk out a sentence. Check.<br />Horrifically stilted sentences. Check.<br />Personality deficient leading lady that the whole world revolves around and who is, without question, sublime in all ways. Check.<br /><br />The entirety of the start of the book was written so badly that I literally cannot bring myself to read any further into this. I can't believe the narrative about the female lead and the entire thing just sounds stilted and obnoxious. <br /><br /><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[
  <i>As usual, Teresa, the platinum blonde with long hair, and Tawny, the longhaired redhead, had half the bar turn in their direction to see what all the fuss was about. That just made the two of them laugh harder, until Teresa suggested Tawny go over and talk to him or he might think they were laughing at him.<br />The girls liked to have fun, but being or seeming to be rude was not something they did. Many visitors to Montréal, upon visiting this friendly bar, had such a great time that they would return if they ever came back to town. Sometimes the two women felt as though they were the un-official ambassadors for the city.</i>
 <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br />I genuinely did not make that up. Everything about this book so far literally makes me want to rip my hair out, however I was too busy snorting with laughter and wishing I could go back and stop myself from purchasing this to get to that stage. How disappointingly awful. </span>

<div id="review_1063966346" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1063966346" />
    <a title="Glenn Trust" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/27747186-glenn-trust"><img alt="Glenn Trust" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1390523827p2/27747186.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1063966346?book_show_action=true">Sep 25, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Glenn Trust" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Glenn Trust" href="/user/show/27747186-glenn-trust">Glenn Trust</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1063966346" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9349219593552420074">As I have said in the past, I read everything, and yes, on occasion I have been known to read erotica, but when I do it is only the best....and Karena Marie is the best.<br/><br/>Why is she the best? Have you ever noticed that many, most even, authors of erotica write as if they are scripting a scene from a C level porn video (Not that I would know anything about porn videos, of course).<br/><br/>Ms. Marie is not a porn writer, she is an author whose specialized niche is erotica. As in all of her books, the most er</span>
  <span id="freeText9349219593552420074" style="display:none">As I have said in the past, I read everything, and yes, on occasion I have been known to read erotica, but when I do it is only the best....and Karena Marie is the best.<br /><br />Why is she the best? Have you ever noticed that many, most even, authors of erotica write as if they are scripting a scene from a C level porn video (Not that I would know anything about porn videos, of course).<br /><br />Ms. Marie is not a porn writer, she is an author whose specialized niche is erotica. As in all of her books, the most erotic part of the book is the reality of her characters and the situations they encounter. There are no silly pretexts leading to the erotic scenes.(Nurses, pool boys, lonely housewives, etc.) Her characters are real, in real situations and that makes all the difference.<br /><br />Sexuality is a part of life, a darned good part if you ask me. In the way that the most terrifying horror stories and thrillers have some basis in reality (Hitchcock's Psycho, and The Rear Window come to mind), for me, the most tantalizing, scintillating erotica comes from the real world.<br /><br />Karena Marie's work is based in reality, and the reality increases the erotic tension of her stories. The Happy Spinster is no exception. Tawny is a believable character, in control of her life and sexuality. Her encounters, while graphic, are believable , making them even more erotic.<br /><br />Yes, I read everything. I like a good story and when I read erotica, I want it based in a lusty reality that I can envision.<br /><br />In short, when I read erotica, I read Karena Marie.<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="9349219593552420074" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_686573621" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/686573621" />
    <a title="Christoph Fischer" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/13998364-christoph-fischer"><img alt="Christoph Fischer" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1473825343p2/13998364.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/686573621?book_show_action=true">Aug 05, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Christoph Fischer" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Christoph Fischer" href="/user/show/13998364-christoph-fischer">Christoph Fischer</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer686573621" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7600636419914151673">"The Happy Spinster" by Karena Marie takes a refreshing and delightful approach to both erotic fiction and female characterisation.<br/>Starting with an excellent clarification of what a "spinster" actually is, the author claims the right for unattached women to be as "non-starved of sex" as is allowed their male counterparts in the societal views.<br/>Her female characters are confident,realistic and fun-filled women with standards yet without pretence. I immediately loved their fresh attitude.<br/>The story </span>
  <span id="freeText7600636419914151673" style="display:none">"The Happy Spinster" by Karena Marie takes a refreshing and delightful approach to both erotic fiction and female characterisation.<br />Starting with an excellent clarification of what a "spinster" actually is, the author claims the right for unattached women to be as "non-starved of sex" as is allowed their male counterparts in the societal views.<br />Her female characters are confident,realistic and fun-filled women with standards yet without pretence. I immediately loved their fresh attitude.<br />The story concerns mainly Tawny, a woman from Montreal, as she sexually encounters Troy from Texas. They are having great sex and a great time. Although I am not a big fan of erotica I found those scenes well written and much better than many I have read, mainly because they were quite naturally embedded in the rest of the story and were not trying to be shocking or boundary breaking. Realistic with some original ideas and written with great passion they are sexy and pleasant to read.<br />The ending is excellent and in my view puts the author in a different league of writers, it is impossible to talk about it without spoiling it for you. With her talent Karena Marie has the potential for a long career ahead of her, both in erotica and in other fiction, should she chose to go there.<br />Very enjoyable. </span>
  <a data-text-id="7600636419914151673" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

    <a title="Alan Hardy" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/13307914-alan-hardy"><img alt="Alan Hardy" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1349397352p2/13307914.jpg" /></a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer624839963" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer119109359145681345">Red-headed Tawny Hudson, aged forty-two, boutique-owner, resident of Montreal, and unmarried, is of the opinion that sexual variety is the spice of life. She is an independent-minded, self-assured woman very much at ease with her sexuality and unafraid to indulge her desires; she feels no need to look for anything beyond the immediate sexual gratification of the moment. Her life is a series of no-strings-attached relationships and one-night stands. Scruples, though, she does have: she will not k</span>
  <span id="freeText119109359145681345" style="display:none">Red-headed Tawny Hudson, aged forty-two, boutique-owner, resident of Montreal, and unmarried, is of the opinion that sexual variety is the spice of life. She is an independent-minded, self-assured woman very much at ease with her sexuality and unafraid to indulge her desires; she feels no need to look for anything beyond the immediate sexual gratification of the moment. Her life is a series of no-strings-attached relationships and one-night stands. Scruples, though, she does have: she will not knowingly have a fling with a married man. The ensuing story concerns her one-night stand with Troy, a visiting Texan, with more than just a big hat. Where normally in her sexual encounters she has been the dominant partner, as indeed she is in her first sexual bout with Troy, graphically and intimately described, she seems to become more passive and submissive with him, allowing him to control and arouse her. We follow them through a series of sex acts and games. Check out what happens. Has Tawny finally been tamed? Or will she turn the tables on Troy? Be prepared to be thrilled, excited and shocked, and then shocked, excited and thrilled again! Tawny is a woman every man will want to devour, or, even better, be devoured by!</span>

<div id="review_978979927" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/978979927" />
    <a title="Candi Silk" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/28511828-candi-silk"><img alt="Candi Silk" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1409875081p2/28511828.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/978979927?book_show_action=true">Jun 27, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Candi Silk" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Candi Silk" href="/user/show/28511828-candi-silk">Candi Silk</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer978979927" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13146592190284471172">The Happy Spinster is drenched with pulse-quickening pleasure!<br/><br/>Tawny Hudson is a dangerous but exciting woman. Why? Because she’s at that point in a woman’s life that’s tantalizingly risky. Risky for herself, and those around her. Tawny is in her early forties, single, and successful by any standards. She’s in that age-zone of having wisdom from past experiences, but still blossoming into full blown maturity with an unleashed eagerness to try new adventures. So anyone hooking up with her exposes </span>
  <span id="freeText13146592190284471172" style="display:none">The Happy Spinster is drenched with pulse-quickening pleasure!<br /><br />Tawny Hudson is a dangerous but exciting woman. Why? Because she’s at that point in a woman’s life that’s tantalizingly risky. Risky for herself, and those around her. Tawny is in her early forties, single, and successful by any standards. She’s in that age-zone of having wisdom from past experiences, but still blossoming into full blown maturity with an unleashed eagerness to try new adventures. So anyone hooking up with her exposes themselves to high-risk involvement. Tawny exudes reckless fun. Could be over-the-edge interesting.<br /><br />And author, Karena Marie, makes it so, as auburn-haired Tawny Hudson from Montreal meets smoky green-eyed Troy from Texas. Sparks fly wildly, and both have their hands full. Literally. As the story unfolds, the full flavor of past hurts and happiness in the background of The Happy Spinster begin to play out. The author knows just how to pull the reader along on Tawny Hudson’s nocturnal adventures. But the stakes increase as the self-assured Tawny is tempted by equally self-assured Troy from Texas. I felt the tangle of temptations as I turned the pages.<br /><br />The author writes with a direct, crisp, style that reflects the determined nature of the protagonist. This is not an ambivalent story, but one that’s on a direct course of pleasure-seeking. And as a reader, I found myself in the middle of the heat-filled encounters of Tawny and Troy. Umm, being in the middle can be exciting!<br /><br />The Happy Spinster is a character-driven tale that is easily carried by protagonist, Tawny Hudson. From page one her confidence moves her on a direct course, heading for exactly what she wants, when she wants it, and from whom. Not an ounce of bashfulness can be found in Tawny’s hungry body or her seductive words. She is very much a woman who’s in control, holding equally “her liquor, and her licker.”<br /><br />Although Tawny and Troy have different cultural and motivational origins, they find an intensely sensuous playground on which to tangle. Both sense a deeper fulfillment, but neither knows just how far and how much they’ll have to give in order to get their final satisfactions. As physical passions sizzle, both Tawny and Troy are challenged by the yonder horizon of the future. As a reader, I like a story spiced with that kind of suspense.<br /><br />The author has primed her first book with a number of possibilities, and it looks as though Tawny Hudson has some stimulating experiences in store as The Happy Spinster series continues. Tawny has demonstrated that she’s ready, willing, and open—in a number of ways—for fulfillment of her desires and wants, and apology is not a word in her vocabulary. She’d pass as an innocent spinster in your neighborhood, but when night shadows fall, she’s on the prowl and all options are on the table. Uh…let’s make that, all options are on the bed. Never underestimate a woman full of passion, entering the gateway to her forties.<br /><br />By the time I finished reading the first volume, my Kindle was panting heavily, and I was too. Thanks, Ms. Marie, for an evening of Five-Star entertainment! Let your suggestive pen continue, as The Happy Spinster entertains your readers.<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="13146592190284471172" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

Lastly, I wish authors would finish a story, then continue making secondary characters the focus of the new sto</span>
  <span id="freeText815860532894315548" style="display:none"><strong>I hate cliffhangers...</strong><br /><br />The premise of this book was good, but didn't deliver. I was disappointed with how immature and irresponsible these 40 years old were.<br /><br />A good editor is needed. Too much dialogue. When giving background information, character development and details, this author is good. <br /><br />Why were they yelling at each other, even when whispering (incorrect use of exclamation points)? Lastly, I wish authors would finish a story, then continue making secondary characters the focus of the new story.<br /><br />All that aside, if you're looking for steamy sex, this book delivers!!</span>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('a0qFh258ZLiiuLBBKOXKF9NwEIZPPTvVJFKZZTjZH5ZF/HBl+pvi4j+RDl8TAyXZt2VX8jdQqJTKz/qG+sjyUA==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('C3YEPb8Q7Y8vriLPni2O+qRsOESjyV8RG6hIssF2ylslwPHfK/dr1bKHnNGly2E0wHl/MNukzFD1NStRA2cnnQ==')})
  }

<span id="freeTextContainer9700406915079031007">Karena Marie is an award winning author of erotica. Her debut novel, The Happy Spinster, was received with mixed reviews as the twists and turns her readers now expect, left some shocked by the ending.   <span id="freeText9700406915079031007" style="display:none">Karena Marie is an award winning author of erotica. Her debut novel, The Happy Spinster, was received with mixed reviews as the twists and turns her readers now expect, left some shocked by the ending. Some readers were upset and considered the ending to be a cliff-hanger. Next published was The Date, where Tawny's adventures continued and concluded in The Choice. All three are now available in the box set, The Happy Spinster Trilogy. Readers love her well written, scorching hot and spicy sex scenes, realistic dialogues that feature strong, sassy, confident women and their hot alpha males in the thrilling biker love story, Lukas, The Barmaid who takes a second chance at love and the award winning Montreal Escort. A prolific writer, several of Karena's stories are currently in various stages of post-production. Look for new releases in 2016 featuring a hunky firefighter and the ladies from Montreal Escort return to discuss some of their hottest adventures in 'Pillow Talk'.</span>
